prefix-set LTE_ROUTES_IN
  0.0.0.0/0 le 32,
  ::/0 le 128
end-set
!
prefix-set WDN_ROUTES_IN
  0.0.0.0/0 le 32
end-set
!
prefix-set LTE_ROUTES_OUT
  2001:4888:2032:3000::/52,
  2001:4888:23f:6200::/56,
  2001:4888:2000:0:3a0:2a0::/112
end-set
!
prefix-set WDN_ROUTES_OUT
  10.182.168.0/24,
  10.249.208.192/27,
  10.249.209.224/28,
  10.205.26.0/28,
  10.205.24.0/23,
  10.222.56.0/21,
  10.245.24.0/23,
  10.120.4.0/23,
  10.120.6.0/23,
  10.120.54.0/23,
  10.120.56.0/22,
  10.244.12.0/23,
  10.244.26.0/23,
  10.205.24.80/30,
  10.205.24.84/30,
  151.144.131.128/26,
  151.144.131.192/26,
  10.208.99.208/30
end-set
!
prefix-set BLOCKED_LTE_ROUTES_IN
  0.0.0.0/0,
  ::/0
end-set
!
prefix-set BLOCKED_WDN_ROUTES_IN
  0.0.0.0/0
end-set
!
community-set LTE_COMMUNITIES
  6167:10998
end-set
!
route-policy LTE_IN
  if destination in BLOCKED_LTE_ROUTES_IN then
    drop
  elseif destination in LTE_ROUTES_IN then
    pass
  else
    drop
  endif
end-policy
!
route-policy WDN_IN
  if destination in BLOCKED_WDN_ROUTES_IN then
    drop
  elseif destination in WDN_ROUTES_IN then
    pass
  else
    drop
  endif
end-policy
!
route-policy LTE_OUT
  if destination in LTE_ROUTES_OUT then
    set community LTE_COMMUNITIES
    pass
  else
    drop
  endif
end-policy
!
route-policy WDN_OUT
  if destination in WDN_ROUTES_OUT then
    pass
  else
    drop
  endif
end-policy
!
route-policy MLDP-INBAND
  set core-tree mldp-inband
end-policy
!
route-policy DENY_ALL_RIP
  drop
end-policy
!
route-policy ADVERTISE_TO_CELL
  if destination in (0.0.0.0/0, ::/0) then
    pass
  else
    drop
  endif
end-policy
!
route-policy RAN_REDIST_STATIC_TO_OSPF
  if tag is 190 then
    drop
  else
    pass
  endif
end-policy
!
